## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the population growth rate (dP/dt) as a function of time (t) and current population size (P). This is a classic population dynamics problem where growth rate depends on population size through various feedback mechanisms such as density dependence, Allee effects, and carrying capacity limitations.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Malthusian/exponential growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Unlimited exponential growth, growth rate proportional to population'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence'}
- {'name': 'Gompertz growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate decreasing logarithmically as population approaches carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Allee effect growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P)', 'scenario': 'Strong Allee effect with minimum viable population threshold'}
- {'name': 'Weak Allee effect', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P)', 'scenario': 'Reduced per-capita growth at low density without extinction threshold'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Asymmetric sigmoidal growth generalization'}
- {'name': 'Von Bertalanffy-type growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Balance between anabolic (power-law) and catabolic (linear) processes'}
- {'name': 'Power-law density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Growth rate as a power function of population size'}
- {'name': 'Quadratic density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2', 'scenario': 'Linear growth with quadratic self-limitation term'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent logistic', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * exp(c2 * t)', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth with time-varying intrinsic growth rate'}
- {'name': 'Beverton-Holt continuous analog', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Saturating reproduction minus density-dependent mortality'}
- {'name': 'Cubic polynomial in P', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3', 'scenario': 'General polynomial density dependence up to third order'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent negative feedback → quadratic term -c*P^2 or rational form P/(1+c*P) limiting growth at high population
- Allee effect (positive density dependence at low P) → cubic polynomial in P with sign changes, or multiplicative factor (P - c_threshold)
- Per-capita growth rate declining linearly with P → dP/dt = r*P*(1 - P/K) logistic structure
- Logarithmic saturation of per-capita rate → Gompertz-type log(K/P) factor multiplying P
- Asymmetric growth curves → power-law exponent on the density-dependent term (theta-logistic)
- Competing growth and mortality processes → difference of power-law terms c0*P^a - c1*P^b
- Time-explicit environmental forcing → multiplicative periodic or exponential function of t modulating growth rate
- Population growth rate vanishing at P=0 → all terms should contain P as a factor (biological consistency)

**GT simplified:**
```
0.11424*(1 - P/40.698)*P + 0.11424*(1 - exp(-0.08368*P))*P + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

Expanding:
```
0.11424*P - 0.11424*P²/40.698 + 0.11424*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P) + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```
```
= -0.002807*P² + 0.22848*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P) + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

The GT has these basis functions:
1. **P²** term
2. **P** term  
3. **P·exp(-αP)** term (where α ≈ 0.08368)
4. **P·exp(-αt)** term

This is crucial: the GT contains `P*exp(-c*P)` and `P*exp(-c*t)` as essential basis functions.

Let me now check each candidate for the presence of these basis functions.

**Key observations for filtering:**
- Need `P*exp(c*P)` type term (exponential in P)
- Need `P*exp(c*t)` type term (exponential in t)
- `sin()` cannot replace `exp()` 
- `log()` cannot replace `exp()`
- Polynomial terms alone cannot match exponentials

**Candidate 13:** `(P³c0+P²c1+Pc2*(P+c3)*exp(c4*t)+Pc5+c6*t+c7)/(P+c3)`
Expanding: P²c0 - Pc0*c3 + c0*c3² + ... wait, let me be more careful.

Dividing by (P+c3):
= P²c0 + P(c1-c0*c3) + (c0*c3²-c1*c3+c5) + Pc2*exp(c4*t) + (c6*t+c7-c3(c0*c3²-c1*c3+c5))/(P+c3) + ...

Actually this is getting complex. Let me do polynomial long division properly.

Numerator = P³c0 + P²c1 + P²c2*exp(c4*t) + Pc2*c3*exp(c4*t) + Pc5 + c6*t + c7

Dividing by (P+c3):
- P³c0/(P+c3) = P²c0 - Pc0*c3 + c0*c3² - c0*c3³/(P+c3)
- P²c1/(P+c3) = Pc1 - c1*c3 + c1*c3²/(P+c3)
- P²c2*exp(c4*t)/(P+c3) = Pc2*exp(c4*t) - c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c2*c3²*exp(c4*t)/(P+c3)
- Pc2*c3*exp(c4*t)/(P+c3) = c2*c3*exp(c4*t) - c2*c3²*exp(c4*t)/(P+c3)
- Pc5/(P+c3) = c5 - c3*c5/(P+c3)
- (c6*t+c7)/(P+c3)

So combining:
= P²c0 + P(-c0*c3+c1) + (c0*c3²-c1*c3+c5) + Pc2*exp(c4*t) + remainder/(P+c3)

Where remainder = -c0*c3³ + c1*c3² - c3*c5 + c6*t + c7

For this to match GT, we need the remainder to be 0 (so no 1/(P+c3) term), and we need:
- P²: c0 (matches GT's P² term ✓)
- P: -c0*c3+c1 (matches GT's P term ✓)
- P*exp(c4*t): this gives P*exp(t) ✓
- But GT needs P*exp(-αP), which is absent here. No match.

Has P²*exp(t), P*exp(t), exp(c4*P), linear t.
GT = -0.002807*P² + 0.22848*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P) + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)

This candidate has exp(c4*P) but GT has P*exp(c*P). These are different: exp(P) vs P*exp(P). Can we get P*exp(P) from this? No, exp(P) and P*exp(P) are linearly independent. No match.

GT has: P²*(const) + P*(const) + P*exp(c*P)*(const) + P*exp(c*t)*(const)

This candidate has P²*exp(t), P*exp(t), P*exp(t)*log(P). The first two terms have exp(t) multiplied, but GT has constant coefficients for P² and P terms. We'd need exp(c1*t) = constant, so c1=0. Then P²c0 + Pc2 + Pc3*exp(c4*t)*log(Pc5+1).
